<Blind Ruins>                               
Ruins buried deep in the jungle. Located in 
a marshy spot with water, water everywhere. 
                                            
<Descent Ruins>                             
Tower-shaped ruins said to be built as an   
ancient astronomical observatory.           
<Heaven Ruins>                              
Wooden tower ruins located deep in a forest.
Lush with moss and mushrooms, it is steadily
merging into the surrounding landscape.     
<Shades Ruins>                              
Ruins located on a cold high plateau.       
Inside, the temperature drops steadily as   
as you descend into the icy rooms.          
<Sheol Ruins>                               
Ruins in a volcanic zone, with molten lava  
everywhere. It was discovered after a       
volcanic eruption a few years ago.
